Emami Limited    EMAMILTD : Updates EMAMILTD : Emami Limited has informed the Exchange regarding 'Emami International FZE, Sharjah, the Wholly Owned Subsidiary
Company of Emami Ltd has disposed its entire stake of 85% held in Fravin Pty Ltd, Australia, consequently, Fravin Pty Ltd and its step down subsidiary companies, namely Diamond Bio Tech Laboratories Pty. Ltd and Abache Pty Ltd have ceased to be subsidiary Companies of
Emami Ltd. 
Fravin Pty Ltd, Diamond Bio Tech Laboratories Pty. Ltd and Abache Pty Ltd were inoperative and there was no contribution in the consolidated revenue/ turnover of Emami Ltd; therefore, there will be no impact on the operations/ financials of the Company.
'.

AstraZeneca Pharma India Limited    ASTRAZEN : Updates ASTRAZEN : AstraZeneca Pharma India Limited has informed the Exchange regarding 'This is to inform that AstraZeneca Pharma India Limited has received Import and Market Permission in Form CT-20 (Marketing Authorization) from the Drugs Controller General of India for Benralizumab 30mg/mL solution for injection (Fasenra ).

Benralizumab (Fasenra ) is indicated as an add-on maintenance treatment for severe asthma with an eosinophilic phenotype in adult patients. 

The receipt of this permission paves way for the launch of Benralizumab (Fasenra ) in India, subject to the receipt of related statutory approvals and licenses. 
'.

Under this partnership, the Company will originate and service the customers through the entire loan life-cycle including sourcing, documentation, collection and loan servicing and in turn ICICI Bank will provide funding to these customers.
 
Definitive Agreements for the said arrangement including the Sourcing Agent Agreement and Service Provider Agreement have been executed between the Company and ICICI Bank on December, 18 2020.

Kindly take the same on record and oblige.
'.

A2Z Infra Engineering Limited    A2ZINFRA : Diversification/Disinvestment Dear Sir,

In compliance with Regulation 30 of SEBI (Listing Obligations and Disclosure Requirements) Regulations, 2015 read with SEBI Circular No. CIR/CFD/CMD/4/2015 dated September 9, 2015, We, A2Z INFRA ENGINEERING LTD. (hereinafter referred as  Company ) wish to inform you that the Board has decided to transfer its 100% stake held in A2Z Powertech Limited ( a Wholly Owned Subsidiary Company of A2Z Infra Engineering Limited ) to A2Z Waste Management (Ludhiana) Ltd., an indirect subsidiary of the Company. Henceforth, A2Z Powertech will cease to be the wholly owned subsidiary of the Company and will become an indirect subsidiary of the Company.
Further the details of the information required to be disclosed under SEBI Circular CIR/CFD/CMD/4/2015 dated September 09, 2015 are provided in Annexure-A attached herewith.

The said information has been uploaded on the website of Stock Exchanges and on the website of the Company at www.a2zgroup.co.in.

You are requested to take the above information on record.
